<div id="page0" style="width:612.0pt;height:792.0pt">
<p style="top:154.0pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:34.4pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:34.4pt;color:#10244f">Simplicity at Scale</span></b></p>
<p style="top:238.6pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:13.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:13.0pt;color:#10244f">Developer teams experiencing rapid growth and success know there are </span></p>
<p style="top:258.6pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:13.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:13.0pt;color:#10244f">obstacles they must face when scaling to meet the demands of users. It can </span></p>
<p style="top:278.6pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:13.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:13.0pt;color:#10244f">be especially challenging to maintain performance and reliability while </span></p>
<p style="top:298.6pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:13.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:13.0pt;color:#10244f">engineering teams expand and users are rapidly acquired. Containerized, </span></p>
<p style="top:318.6pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:13.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:13.0pt;color:#10244f">microservices-oriented applications that leverage the cloud&#x2019;s extensible </span></p>
<p style="top:338.6pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:13.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:13.0pt;color:#10244f">functionality can support teams as they scale, mitigating the adversities that </span></p>
<p style="top:358.6pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:13.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:13.0pt;color:#10244f">arise from accelerated growth. However, Cloud Native delivery pipelines </span></p>
<p style="top:378.6pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:13.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:13.0pt;color:#10244f">come with their own challenges and require investments in DevOps </span></p>
<p style="top:398.6pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:13.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:13.0pt;color:#10244f">processes and systems that can often pose signi&#xfb01;cant hurdles. In offering a </span></p>
<p style="top:418.6pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:13.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:13.0pt;color:#10244f">managed platform for running containerized applications, DigitalOcean </span></p>
<p style="top:438.6pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:13.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:13.0pt;color:#10244f">Kubernetes empowers development teams to spend less time worrying </span></p>
<p style="top:458.6pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:13.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:13.0pt;color:#10244f">about provisioning and operating cloud infrastructure and more time </span></p>
<p style="top:478.6pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:13.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:13.0pt;color:#10244f">building powerful, scalable, and resilient applications.</span></p>

<p style="top:133.9pt;left:71.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">Executive Summary</span></b></p>
<p style="top:152.9pt;left:71.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">Trends in Modern Application Development</span></b></p>
<p style="top:171.9pt;left:71.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f"> </span></b></p>
<p style="top:171.9pt;left:107.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">Twelve Factor</span></p>
<p style="top:190.9pt;left:71.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">Cloud Native</span></b></p>

<p style="top:209.9pt;left:107.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">Scaling with Kubernetes Case Study: The Snappy Monolith</span></p>
<p style="top:228.9pt;left:71.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">Microservices</span></b></p>
<p style="top:247.9pt;left:71.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f"> </span></p>
<p style="top:247.9pt;left:107.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">Breaking the Monolith: Snappy Microservices Architecture</span></p>
<p style="top:266.9pt;left:71.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">Containers</span></b></p>
<p style="top:285.9pt;left:71.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f"> </span></p>
<p style="top:285.9pt;left:107.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">Building a Snappy Microservice: Web UI Container Lifecycle</span></p>
<p style="top:304.9pt;left:71.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">Clusters</span></b></p>
<p style="top:323.9pt;left:71.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">Kubernetes</span></b></p>
<p style="top:342.9pt;left:71.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f"> </span></p>
<p style="top:342.9pt;left:107.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">Kubernetes Design Overview</span></p>
<p style="top:361.9pt;left:71.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">DigitalOcean Kubernetes</span></b></p>
<p style="top:380.9pt;left:71.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f"> </span></p>
<p style="top:380.9pt;left:107.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">Completing the Shift to Cloud Native: Snappy on DigitalOcean Kubernetes</span></p>
<p style="top:134.8pt;left:530.3pt;line-height:10.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">03</span></b></p>
<p style="top:153.8pt;left:530.3pt;line-height:10.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">05</span></b></p>
<p style="top:172.8pt;left:530.3pt;line-height:10.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">05</span></b></p>
<p style="top:191.8pt;left:529.9pt;line-height:10.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">06</span></b></p>
<p style="top:210.8pt;left:530.6pt;line-height:10.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">07</span></b></p>
<p style="top:229.8pt;left:529.8pt;line-height:10.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">08</span></b></p>
<p style="top:248.8pt;left:529.9pt;line-height:10.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">09</span></b></p>
<p style="top:267.8pt;left:534.6pt;line-height:10.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">11</span></b></p>
<p style="top:286.8pt;left:532.9pt;line-height:10.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">13</span></b></p>
<p style="top:305.8pt;left:532.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">16</span></b></p>
<p style="top:324.8pt;left:530.6pt;line-height:10.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">20</span></b></p>
<p style="top:343.8pt;left:530.6pt;line-height:10.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">20</span></b></p>
<p style="top:362.8pt;left:531.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">23</span></b></p>
<p style="top:381.8pt;left:531.1pt;line-height:10.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">24</span></b></p>
<p style="top:484.4pt;left:106.5pt;line-height:12.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:12.0pt;color:#10244f">About DigitalOcean</span></b></p>
<p style="top:511.0pt;left:106.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">DigitalOcean is a cloud services platform delivering the simplicity developers love </span></p>
<p style="top:528.0pt;left:106.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">and businesses trust to run production applications at scale. It provides highly </span></p>
<p style="top:545.0pt;left:106.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">available, secure and scalable compute, storage and networking solutions that help </span></p>
<p style="top:562.0pt;left:106.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">developers build great software faster. Founded in 2012 with of&#xfb01;ces in New York and </span></p>
<p style="top:579.0pt;left:106.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">Cambridge, MA, DigitalOcean offers transparent and affordable pricing, an elegant </span></p>
<p style="top:596.0pt;left:106.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">user interface, and one of the largest libraries of open source resources available. For </span></p>
<p style="top:613.0pt;left:106.5pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">more information, please visit </span><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#0069ff">digitalocean.com</span></b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f"> or follow </span><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#0069ff">@digitalocean</span></b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f"> on Twitter.</span></p>
</div>
<div id="page0" style="width:612.0pt;height:792.0pt">
<p style="top:665.1pt;left:73.3pt;line-height:8.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:8.0pt;color:#a2a2a2">1</span><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:9.0pt;color:#a2a2a2"> Cloud Native Computing Foundation. &#x201c;Kubernetes Is First CNCF Project To Graduate.&#x201d; Cloud Native                      </span></p>
<p style="top:676.3pt;left:73.3pt;line-height:9.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:9.0pt;color:#a2a2a2"> Computing Foundation Blog, Mar. 2018.</span></p>
<p style="top:753.3pt;left:548.8pt;line-height:9.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:9.0pt;color:#10244f">03</span></p>
<p style="top:87.0pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:20.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:20.0pt;color:#10244f">Executive Summary</span></b></p>
<p style="top:129.0pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">In today&#x2019;s fast-moving software landscape, advances in operations technologies have fostered the </span></p>
<p style="top:146.0pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">dramatic reduction of application release cycles. Traditionally, software releases follow a </span></p>
<p style="top:163.0pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">time-based schedule, but it has become increasingly common to see applications and services </span></p>
<p style="top:180.0pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">continuously delivered and deployed to users throughout the day. This truncating of the traditional </span></p>
<p style="top:197.0pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">software release cycle has its roots both in technological developments &#x2014; such as the explosive </span></p>
<p style="top:214.0pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">growth of cloud platforms, containers, and microservices-oriented architectures &#x2014; as well as </span></p>
<p style="top:231.0pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">cultural developments &#x2014; with tech-savvy and mobile-enabled users increasingly expecting new </span></p>
<p style="top:248.0pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">features, fast bug &#xfb01;xes, and a responsive and continuously developing product.</span></p>
<p style="top:282.0pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">This symbiotic relationship between end users and developers has become increasingly linked. </span></p>
<p style="top:299.0pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">Shifting organizational structures and application architectures allow developers to quickly </span></p>
<p style="top:316.0pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">incorporate feedback and react to user demands. This accelerated development cadence often </span></p>
<p style="top:333.0pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">accompanies the packaging of applications into containers, and the use of systems that automate </span></p>
<p style="top:350.0pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">their deployment and orchestration, like Docker Swarm, Marathon, and Kubernetes. These </span></p>
<p style="top:367.0pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">open-source platforms, now stable enough for large-scale production deployments, allow service </span></p>
<p style="top:384.0pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">owners to launch and scale applications themselves, effortlessly managing hundreds of </span></p>
<p style="top:401.0pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">running containers.</span></p>
<p style="top:450.4pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:12.0pt"><b><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:12.0pt;color:#10244f">Kubernetes and DigitalOcean Kubernetes</span></b></p>
<p style="top:477.0pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">Kubernetes, initially open-sourced by Google in 2014, has today grown to become one of the </span></p>
<p style="top:494.0pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">highest velocity projects on GitHub, with over 11,300 contributing developers and 75,000 commits.</span><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:8.0pt;color:#10244f">1</span><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f"> </span></p>
<p style="top:511.0pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">The growth of its thriving open-source community mirrors its popularity in the private sector, with </span></p>
<p style="top:528.0pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">over 50% of Fortune 100 companies relying on Kubernetes every day to rapidly deploy new </span></p>
<p style="top:545.0pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">features and bug &#xfb01;xes to users.</span><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:8.0pt;color:#10244f">2</span></p>
<p style="top:579.0pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">DigitalOcean Kubernetes enables development teams both small and large to quickly take </span></p>
<p style="top:596.0pt;left:71.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">advantage of this market-leading container orchestration platform without the lead time required </span></p>
<p style="top:754.6pt;left:267.2pt;line-height:7.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:7.0pt;color:#10244f">RUNNING CLOUD NATIVE APPLICATIONS ON DIGITALOCEAN KUBERNETES</span></p>
<p style="top:692.3pt;left:73.3pt;line-height:8.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:8.0pt;color:#a2a2a2">2</span><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:9.0pt;color:#a2a2a2"> RedMonk. &#x201c;Cloud Native Technologies in the Fortune 100.&#x201d; RedMonk Charting Stacks, Sept. 2017.</span></p>
</div>
<div id="page0" style="width:612.0pt;height:792.0pt">
<p style="top:753.3pt;left:576.7pt;line-height:9.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:9.0pt;color:#10244f">04</span></p>
<p style="top:85.8pt;left:72.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">to provision, install, and operate a cluster. With its simplicity and developer-friendly interfaces, </span></p>
<p style="top:102.8pt;left:72.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">DigitalOcean Kubernetes empowers developers to launch their containerized applications into a </span></p>
<p style="top:119.8pt;left:72.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">managed, production-ready cluster without having to maintain and con&#xfb01;gure the underlying </span></p>
<p style="top:136.8pt;left:72.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">infrastructure. Seamlessly integrating with the rest of the DigitalOcean suite &#x2014; including Load </span></p>
<p style="top:153.8pt;left:72.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">Balancers, Firewalls, Object Storage Spaces, and Block Storage Volumes &#x2014; and with built-in </span></p>
<p style="top:170.8pt;left:72.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">support for public and private image registries like Docker Hub and Quay.io, developers can now </span></p>
<p style="top:187.8pt;left:72.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">run and scale container-based workloads with ease on the DigitalOcean platform.</span></p>
<p style="top:221.8pt;left:72.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">With full programmatic control of their cluster using the exposed Kubernetes REST API, </span></p>
<p style="top:238.8pt;left:72.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">developers can bene&#xfb01;t from the rich ecosystem of open-source tools while still reaping the </span></p>
<p style="top:255.8pt;left:72.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">convenience of managed infrastructure. Teams can flexibly deploy and scale their Cloud Native </span></p>
<p style="top:272.8pt;left:72.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">applications. A Certi&#xfb01;ed Kubernetes conformant platform, DigitalOcean Kubernetes helps </span></p>
<p style="top:289.8pt;left:72.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">developers launch their application containers and bring their Kubernetes workloads into the </span></p>
<p style="top:306.8pt;left:72.4pt;line-height:10.0pt"><span style="font-family:Sailec,serif;font-size:10.0pt;color:#10244f">DigitalOcean cloud with minimal con&#xfb01;guration and operations overhead.</span></p>
